### BREAKING CHANGES

* **contract:** Officer contract initialization and deployment flow has changed

- Refactor Officer contract to use dynamic beacon configuration
- Add comprehensive NatSpec documentation
- Implement flexible contract deployment via BeaconProxy
- Improve type safety and error handling
- Restructure contract storage to use mapping for beacons
- Add new events for contract deployment and beacon configuration
- Enhance test coverage with structured test suites

Key changes:
- Replace individual beacon addresses with contractBeacons mapping
- Add BeaconConfig struct for initialization
- Implement configureBeacon function for dynamic beacon management
- Add proper input validation for beacon configuration
- Restructure deployContract to deployBeaconProxy with improved flexibility
- Remove direct contract address storage
- Add comprehensive test cases covering all major functionality

### BREAKING CHANGES

* **contract:** Officer contract initialization and deployment flow has changed

* Refactor Officer contract to use dynamic beacon configuration
* Add comprehensive NatSpec documentation
* Implement flexible contract deployment via BeaconProxy
* Improve type safety and error handling
* Restructure contract storage to use mapping for beacons
* Add new events for contract deployment and beacon configuration
* Enhance test coverage with structured test suites

Key changes:

* Replace individual beacon addresses with contractBeacons mapping
* Add BeaconConfig struct for initialization
* Implement configureBeacon function for dynamic beacon management
* Add proper input validation for beacon configuration
* Restructure deployContract to deployBeaconProxy with improved flexibility
* Remove direct contract address storage
* Add comprehensive test cases covering all major functionality
